function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }
function err($str) { die("FATAL ERROR: $str\n"); }

	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != 'bad189a3f6198186d66b3763812cae338697871e') {

	}

	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'bad189a3f6198186d66b3763812cae338697871e') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '026bf32d87cca4c2fed3c03b293abee85cd62260') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');

			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'bad189a3f6198186d66b3763812cae338697871e') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/oid_utils.inc.php');
	writefile_8();
	if (!is_file('includes/oid_utils.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/oid_utils.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/oid_utils.inc.php') != '084805c673620f0f1624ebdd0ea44cce474d4b0b') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/oid_utils.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/oid_utils.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/oid_utils.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/oid_utils.inc.php') !== '084805c673620f0f1624ebdd0ea44cce474d4b0b') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oid_utils.inc.php') !== '2f046b8b5addce0bc80d6e053c9884ce492b1302') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/oid_utils.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/oid_utils.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/oid_utils.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/oid_utils.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_8();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oid_utils.inc.php') !== '084805c673620f0f1624ebdd0ea44cce474d4b0b') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/oid_utils.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('oidplus_base.css')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: oidplus_base.css');
	writefile_9();
	if (!is_file('oidplus_base.css')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): oidplus_base.css');
	} else if (sha1_file('oidplus_base.css') != '307e3b0427aa6bfc341fac7b9a66f432f3cb86a5') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): oidplus_base.css');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('oidplus_base.css', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of oidplus_base.css');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('oidplus_base.css') !== '307e3b0427aa6bfc341fac7b9a66f432f3cb86a5') {
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus_base.css') !== '261c7ba119ef404915740ebc665bffea8b9b7a8c') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: oidplus_base.css');
			$tmp = pathinfo('oidplus_base.css');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('oidplus_base.css')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('oidplus_base.css', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_9();
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus_base.css') !== '307e3b0427aa6bfc341fac7b9a66f432f3cb86a5') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): oidplus_base.css');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('oidplus_base.js')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: oidplus_base.js');
	writefile_10();
	if (!is_file('oidplus_base.js')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): oidplus_base.js');
	} else if (sha1_file('oidplus_base.js') != 'b9503e959bc5d617b81832978ce6ae7e4f141549') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): oidplus_base.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('oidplus_base.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of oidplus_base.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('oidplus_base.js') !== 'b9503e959bc5d617b81832978ce6ae7e4f141549') {
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus_base.js') !== '6492954bfa40ea7d49f2fe5852f5043dd8170bd5') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: oidplus_base.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('oidplus_base.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('oidplus_base.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('oidplus_base.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_10();
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus_base.js') !== 'b9503e959bc5d617b81832978ce6ae7e4f141549') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): oidplus_base.js');
		}
	}
}

	writefile_15();
	if (!is_file('plugins/publicPages/090_login/manifest.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/publicPages/090_login/manifest.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/090_login/manifest.xml') != '1513dc39c24d12b8dded84174aff6ec14ae4c79f') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/090_login/manifest.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/publicPages/090_login/manifest.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/publicPages/090_login/manifest.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/090_login/manifest.xml') !== '1513dc39c24d12b8dded84174aff6ec14ae4c79f') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/090_login/manifest.xml') !== '936a7ebc0a3a3d18c0dc73e7d4cd099bd9e256a7') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/publicPages/090_login/manifest.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/publicPages/090_login/manifest.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/publicPages/090_login/manifest.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/publicPages/090_login/manifest.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_15();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/090_login/manifest.xml') !== '1513dc39c24d12b8dded84174aff6ec14ae4c79f') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/090_login/manifest.xml');
		}
	}
}
